SELECT [s0].[Id], [s0].[Address1], [s0].[Address2], [s0].[Age], [s0].[Balance], [s0].[DateOfBirth], [s0].[DeleteAt], [s0].[DeleteBy], [s0].[FirstName], [s0].[Surname], [s0].[SId], [s0].[Status], [s1].[Id], [s1].[CourseId], [s1].[StudentId], [s1].[Id0], [s1].[CreateAt], [s1].[CreateBy], [s1].[DeleteAt], [s1].[DeleteBy], [s1].[Name], [s1].[StartDate], [s1].[Status], [s1].[UpdateAt], [s1].[UpdateBy]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [s].[Id], [s].[Address1], [s].[Address2], [s].[Age], [s].[Balance], [s].[DateOfBirth], [s].[DeleteAt], [s].[DeleteBy], [s].[FirstName], [s].[Surname], [s].[SId], [s].[Status]
    FROM [Students] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND [s].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [s0]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[CourseId], [c].[StudentId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreateAt], [c0].[CreateBy], [c0].[DeleteAt], [c0].[DeleteBy], [c0].[Name], [c0].[StartDate], [c0].[Status], [c0].[UpdateAt], [c0].[UpdateBy]
    FROM [CourseStudent] AS [c]
    INNER JOIN [Course] AS [c0] ON [c].[CourseId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [s1] ON [s0].[Id] = [s1].[StudentId]
ORDER BY [s0].[Id], [s1].[Id]
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3
ORDER BY [s].[Id] DESC

    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY

    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[Age], [s].[Balance], [s].[FirstName], [s].[Surname], [s].[SId]
    FROM [Students] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3
    ORDER BY [s].[Balance], [s].[Age]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [s1]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s1].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
ORDER BY [s1].[Balance], [s1].[Age]
SELECT [c].[Id] AS [CourseId], [c].[Name] AS [CourseName], [c].[StartDate]
FROM [Course] AS [c]
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%thun%')
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%t%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%t%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%t%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%t%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%t%')
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%thun nguyn%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%thun nguyn%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%thun nguyn%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%thun nguyn%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%thun nguyn%')

WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%20%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%20%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%20%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%20%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%20%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%tui%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%tui%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%tui%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%tui%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%tui%')
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%thun%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%p%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%p%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%p%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%p%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%p%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%trai%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%trai%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%trai%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%trai%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%trai%')
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%1%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%1%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%1%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%1%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%1%')
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%2%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%2%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%2%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%2%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%2%')
SELECT [s].[Id], COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'') AS [FullName], [s].[Age], [s0].[Name] AS [SchoolName], [s].[Balance]
FROM [Students] AS [s]
INNER JOIN [School] AS [s0] ON [s].[SId] = [s0].[Id]
WHERE [s].[Status] <> 3 AND (LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Id])) LIKE '%3%' OR LOWER(COALESCE([s].[FirstName], N'') + N' ' + COALESCE([s].[Surname], N'')) LIKE N'%3%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(11), [s].[Age])) LIKE '%3%' OR LOWER([s0].[Name]) LIKE N'%3%' OR LOWER(CONVERT(varchar(100), [s].[Balance])) LIKE '%3%')
